 The eighty ghat of Banaras has now become like the Chowpatty of Mumbai
 yahaan sirf 'subahe banaras main bhor kaa sangeet' hi nahin balki shaam ko bhi sangeet kii dhun gunjane lagi he
 But this music is for the small children who are participating in the summer camp started in the name of Girja Devi here
 assi ghat par is tarah kaa ye pehla samar camp he jahaan bacchon ko nrity, gayan, painting, judo, jaise class chal rahe hai, jisamen badi sankhya main bacchon ke saath unke mata-pita bhi hissaa le rahe hai
 And all this has happened after the removal of the frozen soil at Assi Ghat
 isaki shuruyaat beete navambar maheene main pradhanmantri narendra modi ne assi ghat par fawda chalaakar kiya tha
 This summer camp begins every evening with the lyrics of the song, 'ganga Reti Par Bangla Chhaye The More Raja Chhavi The More Raja' This Dadra song is from the Banaras Gharana, which Girja Devi sings with great heart
 lihaaja unhi kaa ye priy geet ye bachche unheen ke naam par shuru hue ganga kinare assi ghat ke samar camp main na sirf sikh rahe hai balki 12 june ko camp ke samaapan ke din unke saamne gaakar bhi sunaayenge
 This is the first summer camp of its kind at Assi Ghat, where children are being taught various disciplines
 samar camp kii aayojak ankitha khatri kahati hai, ye ek greeshmakaleen shivi girizaa devi ke naam par shuru kiya gaya he or yahaan kareeb 300 mahilaayein va bachche bhaag le rahe hai
 All these are taking training in painting, dance, singing and singing
 ganga ke dwaar par agar bachche ganga ke geet ke bol sikh rahe hai to ganga kii laharon ke mouj se rache-page gaanon ke bol par thirak bhi rahe hai
 This activity is happening at one corner of Assi Ghat
 duusare kone par marshall art ke saath bachche pencil or kaagaj par apane bal man ke sketch ko khinch rahe hai
 The highest confidence is coming from the class of anchoring among children
 ankaring sikh rahe aath saal ke arsh treepathi bataate he ki ham logon ko abhi confidence spiking or dictionari ke bare main bataaya ja rahaa, taaki ham log apana confidence develop kar saken or agar mike ham logon ko mili to ham nervas naa hon
 The comments assi ghat par mitti hatane ke baad pehle subah kii aarti ke saath bhor kaa raag shuru haa or ab isamen shaam ko ye samar camp kii gatividhi jud gai he
 The camp has started from 14 May and will run till 12 June
 5 june se khud girija devi yahaan aakar rose bacchon ko sikhaaengi
 After the changed form of Assi Ghat, many people from not only the city but also from outside have started coming here and the evening's view has become like Chowpatty in Mumbai
 is camp main sirf bachche hi nahin balki bade bhi puri siddat ke saath shaamil ho rahe hai
 Seeing this, you can say that after a mild jubilee of Prime Minister Narendra Modi, such music of life has started flowing in this eighty ghat of Benares not only in the morning but also in the evening that it is just waiting that every attempt of Benares At the ghat, where such beautiful and seductive music is heard
